Log:
Apply patch "revive mac support, initial changes" by Commander.
Closes mantis: #771

The main changes in this:
 - Update the XCode project file
 - Change declaration of unsigned int to GLuint in apropriate places.
 - Disabled the outdated QuickTime image loader. Will use DevIL instead

Wrt other operating systems, the changes do not change any
runtime thing, only compile time things.
